-- -----------------------------------------------------
-- Schema blockbust

-- -----------------------------------------------------
-- Schema blockbust
-- -----------------------------------------------------
CREATE SCHEMA IF NOT EXISTS `blockbust` DEFAULT CHARACTER SET utf8mb4 COLLATE utf8mb4_0900_ai_ci ;
USE `blockbust` ;

-- -----------------------------------------------------
-- Table `blockbust`.`actor`
-- -----------------------------------------------------
CREATE TABLE IF NOT EXISTS `blockbust`.`actor` (
  `actor_id` INT NOT NULL AUTO_INCREMENT,
  `first_name` VARCHAR(45) NULL,
  `last_name` VARCHAR(45) NULL,
  `full_name` VARCHAR(100) NULL,
  PRIMARY KEY (`actor_id`))
ENGINE = InnoDB;


-- -----------------------------------------------------
-- Table `blockbust`.`language`
-- -----------------------------------------------------
CREATE TABLE IF NOT EXISTS `blockbust`.`language` (
  `language_id` INT NOT NULL AUTO_INCREMENT,
  `name` VARCHAR(45) NULL,
  PRIMARY KEY (`language_id`))
ENGINE = InnoDB;


-- -----------------------------------------------------
-- Table `blockbust`.`category`
-- -----------------------------------------------------
CREATE TABLE IF NOT EXISTS `blockbust`.`category` (
  `category_id` INT NOT NULL AUTO_INCREMENT,
  `name` VARCHAR(45) NULL,
  PRIMARY KEY (`category_id`))
ENGINE = InnoDB;


-- -----------------------------------------------------
-- Table `blockbust`.`film`
-- -----------------------------------------------------
CREATE TABLE IF NOT EXISTS `blockbust`.`film` (
  `film_id` INT NOT NULL AUTO_INCREMENT,
  `title` VARCHAR(1000) NULL,
  `description` VARCHAR(10000) NULL,
  `release_year` YEAR(4) NULL,
  `language_id` INT NOT NULL,
  `rental_duration` INT NULL,
  `rental_rate` FLOAT NULL,
  `length` INT NULL,
  `replacement_cost` FLOAT NULL,
  `rating` VARCHAR(45) NULL,
  `special_features` VARCHAR(1000) NULL,
  `category_id` INT NOT NULL,
  PRIMARY KEY (`film_id`, `language_id`, `category_id`),
  INDEX `fk_film_language1_idx` (`language_id` ASC) VISIBLE,
  INDEX `fk_film_category1_idx` (`category_id` ASC) VISIBLE,
  CONSTRAINT `fk_film_language1`
    FOREIGN KEY (`language_id`)
    REFERENCES `blockbust`.`language` (`language_id`)
    ON DELETE NO ACTION
    ON UPDATE NO ACTION,
  CONSTRAINT `fk_film_category1`
    FOREIGN KEY (`category_id`)
    REFERENCES `blockbust`.`category` (`category_id`)
    ON DELETE NO ACTION
    ON UPDATE NO ACTION)
ENGINE = InnoDB;


-- -----------------------------------------------------
-- Table `blockbust`.`store`
-- -----------------------------------------------------
CREATE TABLE IF NOT EXISTS `blockbust`.`store` (
  `store_id` INT NOT NULL AUTO_INCREMENT,
  `address` VARCHAR(1000) NULL,
  `city` VARCHAR(45) NULL,
  `state` VARCHAR(45) NULL,
  `zip` VARCHAR(45) NULL,
  PRIMARY KEY (`store_id`))
ENGINE = InnoDB;


-- -----------------------------------------------------
-- Table `blockbust`.`staff`
-- -----------------------------------------------------
CREATE TABLE IF NOT EXISTS `blockbust`.`staff` (
  `staff_id` INT NOT NULL AUTO_INCREMENT,
  `first_name` VARCHAR(45) NULL,
  `last_name` VARCHAR(45) NULL,
  `position` VARCHAR(45) NULL,
  `store_id` INT NOT NULL,
  PRIMARY KEY (`staff_id`, `store_id`),
  INDEX `fk_staff_store1_idx` (`store_id` ASC) VISIBLE,
  CONSTRAINT `fk_staff_store1`
    FOREIGN KEY (`store_id`)
    REFERENCES `blockbust`.`store` (`store_id`)
    ON DELETE NO ACTION
    ON UPDATE NO ACTION)
ENGINE = InnoDB;


-- -----------------------------------------------------
-- Table `blockbust`.`inventory`
-- -----------------------------------------------------
CREATE TABLE IF NOT EXISTS `blockbust`.`inventory` (
  `inventory_id` INT NOT NULL AUTO_INCREMENT,
  `film_id` INT NOT NULL,
  `store_id` INT NOT NULL,
  `last_update` DATE NULL,
  PRIMARY KEY (`inventory_id`, `film_id`, `store_id`),
  INDEX `fk_inventory_store1_idx` (`store_id` ASC) VISIBLE,
  INDEX `fk_inventory_film1_idx` (`film_id` ASC) VISIBLE,
  CONSTRAINT `fk_inventory_store1`
    FOREIGN KEY (`store_id`)
    REFERENCES `blockbust`.`store` (`store_id`)
    ON DELETE NO ACTION
    ON UPDATE NO ACTION,
  CONSTRAINT `fk_inventory_film1`
    FOREIGN KEY (`film_id`)
    REFERENCES `blockbust`.`film` (`film_id`)
    ON DELETE NO ACTION
    ON UPDATE NO ACTION)
ENGINE = InnoDB;


-- -----------------------------------------------------
-- Table `blockbust`.`customers`
-- -----------------------------------------------------
CREATE TABLE IF NOT EXISTS `blockbust`.`customers` (
  `customer_id` INT NOT NULL AUTO_INCREMENT,
  `first_name` VARCHAR(45) NULL,
  `last_name` VARCHAR(45) NULL,
  `address` VARCHAR(1000) NULL,
  `phone` VARCHAR(45) NULL,
  `email` VARCHAR(100) NULL,
  PRIMARY KEY (`customer_id`))
ENGINE = InnoDB;


-- -----------------------------------------------------
-- Table `blockbust`.`rental`
-- -----------------------------------------------------
CREATE TABLE IF NOT EXISTS `blockbust`.`rental` (
  `rental_id` INT NOT NULL AUTO_INCREMENT,
  `rental_date` DATE NULL,
  `return_date` DATE NULL,
  `inventory_id` INT NOT NULL,
  `customer_id` INT NOT NULL,
  `status` VARCHAR(45) NULL,
  `staff_id` INT NOT NULL,
  `last_update` DATE NULL,
  `days_left` INT NULL,
  PRIMARY KEY (`rental_id`, `inventory_id`, `customer_id`, `staff_id`),
  INDEX `fk_rental_inventory1_idx` (`inventory_id` ASC) VISIBLE,
  INDEX `fk_rental_staff1_idx` (`staff_id` ASC) VISIBLE,
  INDEX `fk_rental_customers1_idx` (`customer_id` ASC) VISIBLE,
  CONSTRAINT `fk_rental_inventory1`
    FOREIGN KEY (`inventory_id`)
    REFERENCES `blockbust`.`inventory` (`inventory_id`)
    ON DELETE NO ACTION
    ON UPDATE NO ACTION,
  CONSTRAINT `fk_rental_staff1`
    FOREIGN KEY (`staff_id`)
    REFERENCES `blockbust`.`staff` (`staff_id`)
    ON DELETE NO ACTION
    ON UPDATE NO ACTION,
  CONSTRAINT `fk_rental_customers1`
    FOREIGN KEY (`customer_id`)
    REFERENCES `blockbust`.`customers` (`customer_id`)
    ON DELETE NO ACTION
    ON UPDATE NO ACTION)
ENGINE = InnoDB;


-- -----------------------------------------------------
-- Table `blockbust`.`film_cast`
-- -----------------------------------------------------
CREATE TABLE IF NOT EXISTS `blockbust`.`film_cast` (
  `actor_id` INT NOT NULL,
  `film_id` INT NOT NULL,
  INDEX `fk_film_has_actor_actor1_idx` (`actor_id` ASC) VISIBLE,
  INDEX `fk_film_has_actor_film1_idx` (`film_id` ASC) VISIBLE,
  PRIMARY KEY (`actor_id`, `film_id`),
  CONSTRAINT `fk_film_has_actor_film1`
    FOREIGN KEY (`film_id`)
    REFERENCES `blockbust`.`film` (`film_id`)
    ON DELETE NO ACTION
    ON UPDATE NO ACTION,
  CONSTRAINT `fk_film_has_actor_actor1`
    FOREIGN KEY (`actor_id`)
    REFERENCES `blockbust`.`actor` (`actor_id`)
    ON DELETE NO ACTION
    ON UPDATE NO ACTION)
ENGINE = InnoDB;


SET SQL_MODE=@OLD_SQL_MODE;
SET FOREIGN_KEY_CHECKS=@OLD_FOREIGN_KEY_CHECKS;
SET UNIQUE_CHECKS=@OLD_UNIQUE_CHECKS;
